  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });
      $('span_class_gr-hyperlink_more_filters_span_tip_279').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1387398742?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1387398742" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17135192708001299931">Check out more of my reviews at <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.bookaddicthaven.com'>www.bookaddicthaven.com</a><br/><br/>This book had been sitting on my TBR list for quite a long time. I am a big fan of M. Robinson's work. After reading 'El Diablo', I knew that I needed to read 'The Good Ol' Boys' series. 'Complicate Me' is the first book in that series and it does not disappoint. I loved this angsty, coming of age romance.<br/><br/>Unlike the other books I've read by this author, this isn't a "dark" read. However, don't mistake that for a lack of emotion or tension. W</span>
  <span id="freeText17135192708001299931" style="display:none">Check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a><br /><br />This book had been sitting on my TBR list for quite a long time. I am a big fan of M. Robinson's work. After reading 'El Diablo', I knew that I needed to read 'The Good Ol' Boys' series. 'Complicate Me' is the first book in that series and it does not disappoint. I loved this angsty, coming of age romance.<br /><br />Unlike the other books I've read by this author, this isn't a "dark" read. However, don't mistake that for a lack of emotion or tension. What this book lacks in kink, it makes up for in angst.<br /><br />Alex, aka "Half-pint", grows up in a small, close-knit community. As an only child, she plays with the older sons of her parents' friends. A few years younger, she follows them around everywhere they go and inserts herself into their group. She is "one of the boys" and they look after her.<br /><br />As they grow up, their relationships change. As the boys indulge in their hedonistic desires, Alex becomes "the child" in the background. The boys are older and are discovering girls, beginning to date and explore their sexuality. <br /><br />Alex is prevented from experiencing many of the normal rites of passage as she grows a little older. The boys make sure of that. They protect her fiercely, preventing any romantic inclinations that other boys might have toward Alex. They keep her sheltered, even as they fool around with anything in a skirt.<br /><br />Unlike the other boys, Lucas has never viewed Alex as a sister. They have a special relationship. He is her "Bo". Lucas loves Alex, but knows that she is too young to act on it. The fact that Alex is off-limits is something that he is frequently reminded of by the other boys.<br /><br />Instead, Lucas does what is expected of him. He hooks up with the other girls in town that are his age. Alex is forced to watch as Lucas sows his wild oats all over town. <br /><br />These two never seemed to be able to get on the same page. The timing was never right. Over and over, they broke each others' hearts. It was a sweet torture to read their story.<br /><br />As I listened to their story, I empathized with Alex. M. Robinson did a wonderful job of capturing the essence of young love and first heartbreak. The emotions were raw and so real they were almost tangible. I was immediately transported back to my teenage years, remembering the emotional highs and lows of youth that gradually fade over time with the loss of innocence. <br /><br />There were so many times that I was furious with the decisions that these two made, but I couldn't quit listening. Lucas, in particular, made some insensitive decisions that damaged his relationship with Alex. Despite his claim to be in love with Alex, Lucas spent a lot of time choosing other girls over her. They spent a lot of time hurting one another before they figured things out.<br /><br />I absolutely loved this angsty, emotional, coming of age love story. There was plenty of heartache, but it only made this book all that much more addicting. I fell in love with all of the characters. I will definitely be continuing this series.</span>

<div id="review_1363225262" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1363225262" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1363225262?book_show_action=true">Aug 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1363225262" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2691927614331967986"><b>4 Angsty stars!</b> <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/A5C5C9F5-453B-4D98-AF6F-4234BAB66F59_zpswtsnvivj.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442308127i/16216184._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo A5C5C9F5-453B-4D98-AF6F-4234BAB66F59_zpswtsnvivj.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>M. Robinson knows how to deliver the angst. This isn’t my first book by her, so I was somewhat prepared. <i>Complicate Me</i> is a friends to lovers/second chance romance that was stressful to read, emotional and angsty as all get out. It was also sweet and funny at times and warmed my heart. I loved watching these characters grow up. This book was so much more than a romance and focused on more than the main characters. It was a book about friendship first and foremost. A coming of</span>
  <span id="freeText2691927614331967986" style="display:none"><b>4 Angsty stars!</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/A5C5C9F5-453B-4D98-AF6F-4234BAB66F59_zpswtsnvivj.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442308127i/16216184._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo A5C5C9F5-453B-4D98-AF6F-4234BAB66F59_zpswtsnvivj.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>M. Robinson knows how to deliver the angst. This isn’t my first book by her, so I was somewhat prepared. <i>Complicate Me</i> is a friends to lovers/second chance romance that was stressful to read, emotional and angsty as all get out. It was also sweet and funny at times and warmed my heart. I loved watching these characters grow up. This book was so much more than a romance and focused on more than the main characters. It was a book about friendship first and foremost. A coming of age story about finding out who you are and what you want in life and just maybe finding the love you were always meant to have along the way. <br><br>What happens when you find the love of your life at ten years old? Alex and Lucas- affectionately known as Half-Pint and Bo have known each other since the day Alex was born. They’ve been the best of friends, along with the 3 other boys in their group. Alex has always had a special bond with Lucas who is 2 years her senior. As she gets older, it only intensifies, turing into more. This story starts when she is 10 and he is 12 and spans the next 15 years or so. Alex is not perfect. Lucas is not perfect. Their story is not perfect. But their love is true and it’s real. It’s also raw, messy and complicated. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/711D9996-2C23-40D5-964A-67D7B528CF46_zpsnpmsw50q.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442308127i/16216185._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 711D9996-2C23-40D5-964A-67D7B528CF46_zpsnpmsw50q.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Overall, I loved a lot about this story. It had some five star moments. I’m gonna tell you the reason this wasn't a five for me. There will be spoilers so read at your own risk :) <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Although Stacey’s pregnancy broke my heart- it was the detailed sex scenes between the others in this book that put me off. I kind of knew going in that the H/h weren’t together the whole book, and I figured that they had sex with other people. I was okay with that for the most part, it’s not like they were cheating on each other. I was okay with it, but I did NOT want to read about it. Especially not it detail. That is just my personal preference. Every book is different when it comes to this topic. I feel like since Alex and Lucas were in love with each other every time they were having sex with someone else just broke my heart and turned me off…  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> This story definitely brought out the emotions in me. I went from being happy, to sad, to angry, to livid, to stressed out, to sad again, then to happy again. Their story is one the will stay with me. <br><i>
  <blockquote>I loved her. I knew I loved her, I always have and I always will. She owned every part of me. My heart was hers since before I knew what having her even meant. </blockquote>
</i> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/74F62339-773B-497F-A35F-3B93AD39F4DC_zpsxfjqoewj.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442308127i/16216186._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 74F62339-773B-497F-A35F-3B93AD39F4DC_zpsxfjqoewj.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved the bond that Alex and Lucas shared. Even though both (especially Lucas) infuriated me with their choices, they DID grow up. I can imagine how difficult it would be to find love that young and have everyone going against it. It was fun to see all the boys grow up along the way. I can’t wait for each and every one of their stories. All are interesting in one way or another. <br><br>I feel like this book will be a memorable one. One of those books you can look back on remember how you felt when you read this scene, the characters and how much their actions effected your feelings. This book was long, but it didn’t feel long. The story hooked me in pretty quickly and I read most of the book in one sitting. I know this is going to sound crazy, because of the length of the book… but I almost wish it would have been longer. I wanted more of Alex and Lucas together. Through all the stress of the book (and trust me, there was plenty of it) I was happy with the end. I can’t wait to read about the other boys. And after reading that last page… GAH! I need the next book ASAP! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “I’m not going to tell you it’s always been easy because it hasn’t, but you’ve always been worth it.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/7E22DCAA-2C5B-4445-B2F7-0D862F1CFFCC_zps1cjqgag9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442308127i/16216187._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 7E22DCAA-2C5B-4445-B2F7-0D862F1CFFCC_zps1cjqgag9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1362126743" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1362126743" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1362126743?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1362126743" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14704261180579822712"><b>2.5 “She’s just a girl” STARS</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”Our relationship was filled with what ifs, and maybe somedays… It was complicated. It was messy. It was us.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492286715ra/22502388.gif' width='390' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Well...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492286715ra/22502387.gif' width='390' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/>When an author asks me to ARC a book, I try very hard to take into consideration all the time and heart that they have poured into their finished product. That being said, I started this one and did like prologue (perhaps only part of book the book that I can say I truly liked) and got to 17% and if not for being asked to read this story directly </span>
  <span id="freeText14704261180579822712" style="display:none"><b>2.5 “She’s just a girl” STARS</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”Our relationship was filled with what ifs, and maybe somedays… It was complicated. It was messy. It was us.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492286715ra/22502388.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Well...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492286715ra/22502387.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>When an author asks me to ARC a book, I try very hard to take into consideration all the time and heart that they have poured into their finished product. That being said, I started this one and did like prologue (perhaps only part of book the book that I can say I truly liked) and got to 17% and if not for being asked to read this story directly by the author, that would have been my quitting mark.<br><br>The prologue is interesting, as Lucas is confronting Alexandra on her upcoming marriage to someone else. Thereafter, I was tortured reading way too many pages about very very young characters. Somewhere along the way it should have been mentioned that first 65 percent needed to be condensed because the day to day of a 10 year girl with a crush on her 13 year old guy friend (who’s getting it regularly from same girl from 7th Grade to Senior year of high school) and thinking of this young girl in sexual ways early on, is simply icky for this mom of two daughters. <br> <br><b>
  <i>”Stacey and I weren’t friends, we barely even spoke, but I knew her role in Lucas’s life and she knew mine. End of story.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441818444ra/16155988.gif" width="390" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Half Pint and Bo, that’s their nicknames, are never actually a couple. They are friends within a larger group of boys that have been hanging out since diapers. There’s a lot of outside advice offered, angst, hurt feelings, and double standards. Both characters have long standing relationships with other people as well. <br><br>Lucas and Alex just keep messing up their chances with one another. The author wants us to believe that they are the forever kind of love that just never had it’s shot. I must have missed the part where we experienced how wonderful they are together. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492286715ra/22502386.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Once the characters get out of high school, the story actually moved at a good pace. However during their late teens and twenties they aren’t together either just the typical run ins that involve:<br><br><b>I LOVE YOU BO</b><br><br><b>I LOVE YOU MY BROWN EYED GIRL</b><br><br><b>IT’S TOO LATE FOR US</b><br><br>and repeat...<br><br>The story ends on a happy sappy note, as our couple has come of age and all falls into place, leaving two hearts crushed in their wake. The chances of these two making it after the epilogue to me are slim to none. Since they argue after seconds together and don’t speak for months at a clip throughout the whole book. But hey if you’re a true romantic and not cynical like myself, this whole story maybe a big win for you. <br><br><i>*ARC provided in exchange for an honest review*</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="14704261180579822712" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1371829243" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1371829243" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1371829243?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1371829243" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11660497537751492716"><b>RATING 4.5 STARS</b><br/><br/>Complicate Me is book one in The Good Ol’ Boys series by M. Robinson. This book was generously provided to me in exchange for an honest review.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441647141i/16132761.jpg' alt='Oak Island, NC: ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Alexandra Collins was born and raised in Oak Island, North Carolina. Her four best friends and constant companions were a set of four boys, three of which were two years older than her, the third just one year. Alex was known to them as their ‘Half Pint.’ She went everywhere with them and they thought of her as their little sister. They al</span>
  <span id="freeText11660497537751492716" style="display:none"><b>RATING 4.5 STARS</b><br><br>Complicate Me is book one in The Good Ol’ Boys series by M. Robinson. This book was generously provided to me in exchange for an honest review.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441647141i/16132761.jpg" alt="Oak Island, NC: " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Alexandra Collins was born and raised in Oak Island, North Carolina. Her four best friends and constant companions were a set of four boys, three of which were two years older than her, the third just one year. Alex was known to them as their ‘Half Pint.’ She went everywhere with them and they thought of her as their little sister. They all loved her and protected her. They were her world as she was theirs. But there was one boy in the group that Alex had a special bond with, different than the others. Lucas or to her he was her ‘Bo.’ When she fell down, it was always Bo that bandaged her knee and it was his handlebars she would ride on. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/1246774430rbqjunh-jpg_zpsf35e2b54.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421721376i/13408797._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 1246774430rbqjunh-jpg_zpsf35e2b54.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>As they all grew older, the boys got interested in girls. Bo felt the special bond he shared with Alex but she was eleven at the time. She was a child. And in their eyes, none of them were good enough for their Half Pint. She was their little sister, their responsibility, and that is where it ended.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You’re a good girl, Alexandra. That’s what makes you my Half-Pint. You’re the calm to my storm; it’s always been that way. You’re my refuge.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441647141i/16132762._SY540_.jpg" alt="riding_double: " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As they all grew up, Lucas made so many mistakes and hurt Alex in so many ways. But the love between them was so deep. Still, they danced around what their true feelings were for each other. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441647141i/16132763._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>“The feelings I had, what he provoked and stirred within me, what he always did to me. No one could ever explain or understand what it was. How it happened. No one else could do this. It was only Lucas. Always Lucas. Not one other soul had this pull. On me. On him. On us.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441647141i/16132764._SY540_.jpg" alt="silver shark's tooth necklace.: " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book takes us through their childhood, middle school, high school, then on to college and adult hood. So many mistakes were made. If they only were honest with each other about the depth of their feelings, would it have made a difference? And it wasn’t just them, there were others keeping them apart, each for their own reasons. <br><br><b>
  <i>“We have so many barriers placed in between us and I don’t know how to remove them.”</i>
</b><br><br>I am writing this review right after I finished the book so my emotions are still a mess. I want to warn you that this book will rip your heart out, not just once, but over and over again. Alex and Lucas had pretty much loved each other from birth. But they were kids and kids make mistakes. I won’t lie to you and say that there wasn’t times that I hated Lucas for what he was doing. Just typing out this review is making my eyes burn all over again. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441647141i/16132765._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>When all is said and done, though, these are the characters I am going to think about when I first wake up in the morning for a very long time. This is a beautiful and heart breaking story of love, loss, growing up and figuring out who you are and where you belong. The next book in the series will be about Lucas’s younger sister, Lily and Lucas’s friend, Jacob. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I loved you then, I love you now, I’ll love you always.”</i>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425952445ra/13954015.gif" alt="signature" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11660497537751492716" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1360990530" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1360990530" />
    <a title="Dee Montoya" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya"><img alt="Dee Montoya" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483914811p2/11880024.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1360990530?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dee Montoya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dee Montoya" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya">Dee Montoya</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=beta-read">beta-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=h-o-t">h-o-t</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=hot-alpha-male">hot-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=kick-ass-awesome-heroine">kick-ass-awesome-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1360990530" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13579340538339494744"><b> ***** FIVE STARS*****</b><br/> <i>(ARC kindly provided by author M. Robinson)</i><br/><br/><br/>This book was simply stunning!!! The story is full of angst and so much beauty. Small town setting, friends to lovers romance and not an easy journey but a love so strong, that you'll feel it in every part of your body. <br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/e75faca0-0a43-4d28-a89d-77a479b5f095_zpsxymqchlu.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441301751i/16090680.jpg' alt=' photo e75faca0-0a43-4d28-a89d-77a479b5f095_zpsxymqchlu.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>Alexandra aka Half Pint, grew up amongst boys. She's an only child but was never in need of sibling love, because these boys have always loved and protected her fiercely. Out of the four boys there is Lucas, he</span>
  <span id="freeText13579340538339494744" style="display:none"><b> ***** FIVE STARS*****</b><br> <i>(ARC kindly provided by author M. Robinson)</i><br><br><br>This book was simply stunning!!! The story is full of angst and so much beauty. Small town setting, friends to lovers romance and not an easy journey but a love so strong, that you'll feel it in every part of your body. <br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/e75faca0-0a43-4d28-a89d-77a479b5f095_zpsxymqchlu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441301751i/16090680.jpg" alt=" photo e75faca0-0a43-4d28-a89d-77a479b5f095_zpsxymqchlu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Alexandra aka Half Pint, grew up amongst boys. She's an only child but was never in need of sibling love, because these boys have always loved and protected her fiercely. Out of the four boys there is Lucas, he's always had a special relationship with Alex; his brown eyed girl.<br><br><br><br>The story develops as they all grow up together; from climbing up on trees to, first school dances, puberty, etc... <br><br><br><br>Alex always wanted to be one of the boys. She had the attitude to fight anybody who wanted to treat her like a girl but when she starts to recognize the nature of her feelings for Lucas, she wants nothing more than for him to stop hanging around other girls and notice her.<br><br><br><br>Lucas is a total alpha male and gorgeous. He adores Alex. When he was young he struggled with his feelings for her, but he always thought of her as his. As they all grow up, everyone can see they have a really strong connection that goes beyond friendship.<br><br><br><br> When they become of an appropriate age, the boys still think of Alex as a little sister and they don't want Lucas and his Casanova tendencies hurting Alex. Their parents want them to experience life before trying to change their friendship for a romance. As they say the heart wants what it wants and it's hard for both Lucas and Alex to keep those feeling hidden. As time goes by, everything around them only becomes complicated. <br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/8c522f72-88b7-46e7-bbe0-91ccbd33f092_zpsu8h20w16.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439307761i/15820210.jpg" alt=" photo 8c522f72-88b7-46e7-bbe0-91ccbd33f092_zpsu8h20w16.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>The beauty of this story is how unpredictable it is. The level of angst will keep you at the edge of your seat and most likely you will devour this book in only one day. I loved the complexity of the characters and the intensity in the story. Also the realness of it all gripped my heart.<br><br><br><br>Another wonderful aspect are the friendships, and the family dynamics between all the characters.<br><br><br><br>This book will make you feel like you are in a beautiful summer romance; beach, friends and first kisses. Amazing!!!!!<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/7fc51b85-0ae4-432c-a667-8d10e83bcb08_zpsdivg4rtg.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439307761i/15820211.jpg" alt=" photo 7fc51b85-0ae4-432c-a667-8d10e83bcb08_zpsdivg4rtg.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I always love it when an author ventures outside of their genre, and succeeds. M. Robinson is known for Erotica and that she can write it well but I believe this is her best work yet.<br><br><br>My <i>Complicate Me</i> music playlist:<br>*When You Say Nothing At All by Allison Krauss<br>*It's Complicated by Keith and Renee<br>*She Hates Me by Puddle of Mudd<br>*Storm by Lifehouse <br>*I loved Her First by Heartland<br>*Everything by Lifehouse<br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/image.jpg1_zpsgbvgk2qi.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441511882i/16118321.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg1_zpsgbvgk2qi.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1391423773" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1391423773" />
    <a title="Pam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13865261-pam"><img alt="Pam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374039144p2/13865261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1391423773?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pam" href="/user/show/13865261-pam">Pam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=5">5</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=love-story">love-story</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=sweeter-side">sweeter-side</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=stand-alone">stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=sixty-first-reads">sixty-first-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1391423773" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13438554173034377806"><i>5 hurricane stars</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I loved you then, I love you now, I’ll love you always.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442294602i/16213784._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/><b>Complicate Me</b> is a story that I knew before reading was going to be full of emotion and feelings, but I underestimated how much of a pull I was going to have with Alex and Lucas. I tend to shy away from books where there is a love triangle, and in this while there was a love triangle it was a seriously unbalanced triangle never leaving any doubt just how strong the bond is between Alex and Lucas; that they wer</span>
  <span id="freeText13438554173034377806" style="display:none"><i>5 hurricane stars</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I loved you then, I love you now, I’ll love you always.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442294602i/16213784._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><b>Complicate Me</b> is a story that I knew before reading was going to be full of emotion and feelings, but I underestimated how much of a pull I was going to have with Alex and Lucas. I tend to shy away from books where there is a love triangle, and in this while there was a love triangle it was a seriously unbalanced triangle never leaving any doubt just how strong the bond is between Alex and Lucas; that they were truly meant to be. But as every great love, nothing comes easy... In order to understand, you have to start from the beginning, how it all started and the challenges and complications that were always in their way. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Love shouldn’t hurt this much. All you’ve ever done… is complicate me.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442295776i/16214023.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Alexandra a.k.a Alex a.k.a. Half-Pint</b> always wanted to be one of the boys, her boys, Dylan, Jacob, Austin and most importantly Lucas. Lucas she knew was different, they always have shared a bond so strong, nothing else mattered. Being the youngest and littlest of the bunch, she always had to fight to prove she was one of the guys, treating her like a little sister; protecting her and later on keeping the boys at bay. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>You’re the calm to my storm; it’s always been that way,” he paused to let his words sink in. “You’re my refuge.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442294602i/16213785.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Lucas a.k.a Bo</b> knew from even when his Half-Pint was in her mom's tummy that she was going to be his. Being older he felt more possessive of her than the rest of the guys, she was his responsibility and he took great pride in taking care of her. He would do anything to keep his girl happy no matter how much shit he got from the guys, nothing mattered but her. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He was always the eye of the storm. When we were kids I loved it, I wanted to be pulled into his winds and let him take me wherever he wanted to go. I'd follow him anywhere. But as we got older I realized it was too late for me to seek refuge. He was already my destruction and there was no way to get past the heavy gusts of our complicated love.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442294602i/16213786.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The problem with knowing each other from birth is that we all grow up, all the changes we go through, what we like and what we need. Growing up is confusing as it is, imagine growing up and having feelings you can not understand or make sense of. There is a fear of keeping those you care for close and not wanting anything to change. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>The boy who promised he would never hurt her.<br><br>The boy who swore he would always protect her.<br><br>The boy who vowed he would never let anything happen to her.<br><br>That same boy was me.<br><br>I was the reason she was bawling.<br><br>I was the reason she was hurt.<br><br>I was the reason she was broken.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442294602i/16213787._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their first kiss was the beginning to their end, the beginning of their complicated love... <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>When… when… when… Our relationship was filled with what ifs, and maybe some days… It was complicated. It was messy. It was us.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397512857ra/9285872.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Complicated Me</b> put me through the ringer, I had to bust out my big girl panties for this one, it was so tragically beautiful to read. Like watching a giant train wreck and not being able to do anything about it; it made me mad, upset, frustrated and just downright sad for Alex and Lucas. All they ever wanted was to be together, growing up and old together, but it was always them against the world. Love is not easy or kind, and sometimes you have to lose your way before finding where you belong. There was nothing I wanted more for Alex and Lucas to find their way back to one another. There were times I wanted to scream and yell but in the end I had to remind myself they were young, if adults have a hard time acting like adults why should I expect the teens to know any better. <br><br>This is the first contemporary novel by M .Robinson, and I have to give it to her she never skimps on telling the story. I started this read around 1 1p.m., I was invested from the very first page, and after the prologue my reaction was "Oh fuck this is going to hurt" and I could not put it down. This was told in dual point of view inviting me to grow with them, it is a stand alone read and has an epilogue to make your heart smile, not to mention get you ready for the next couple whose story is dying to be told. I am happy to say this book was worth rocking the zombie look for, after having finished it at 4a.m. and I had such a book high I knew there would be no sleep. I'd definitely recommend this to my friends especially for those who can appreciate a coming of age tale and who believes in soul-mates. <br><br><i>ARC kindly provided by the author, in exchange for an honest review.</i><br> <br>***Quotes above are taken from the ARC version of the book and may differ upon publication.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13438554173034377806" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1382531850" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1382531850" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1382531850?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1382531850" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17631861203724956962">I've thought about my rating and review long and hard but the bottom line is, Complicate Me isn't for me. I love angst. Love it, but for me, I also need character and plot development, and I found it lacking in this book.<br/><br/>I couldn't connect with the writing at all. The prose, the constant use of semicolons and ellipses were distracting. I also couldn't connect with either Alex or Lucas. Their relationship felt juvenile to me. Their reasons for not being together is more annoying than heartbreakin</span>
  <span id="freeText17631861203724956962" style="display:none">I've thought about my rating and review long and hard but the bottom line is, Complicate Me isn't for me. I love angst. Love it, but for me, I also need character and plot development, and I found it lacking in this book.<br /><br />I couldn't connect with the writing at all. The prose, the constant use of semicolons and ellipses were distracting. I also couldn't connect with either Alex or Lucas. Their relationship felt juvenile to me. Their reasons for not being together is more annoying than heartbreaking. I found myself not caring anymore whether they get together or not. And Lucas...he's not much of a hero for me. <br /><br />Surprisingly, the two characters I ended up liking were Stacey and Lily. Stacey was supposed to be the villain but she was one of the only people who called Lucas out on his shit. Same goes for Lily. She's young but she has more brains that her parents, Lucas and their friends combined.<br /><br />I have other issues but that's basically the gist of it. <br /><br /><b>ETA:</b>My original review said Amber, but I'm wrong. It was Stacey. It's fixed now. <br /><br /><br /><i>ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

<div id="review_1649725440" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1649725440" />
    <a title="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books"><img alt="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528808758p2/37314676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1649725440?book_show_action=true">May 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" href="/user/show/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books">NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books?shelf=romance-young-adult-etc">romance-young-adult-etc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1649725440" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6375479179933243466"><b>
  <i>***5 "<u>My Brown Eyed Girl</u>" stars***</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465644461i/19383752._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>OMG!!! This book wrecked me, but i think that it will stay with me for a long time!!!<br/>It was so difficult to witness this love...<br/>It started at very young age and all those obstacles that were standing on their way were making my heart bleeding!!!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383753.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Alex and Lucas hurt each other very much and my heart was breaking for them...<br/>They left other things to complicate their love and at the end they just making one mistake after the other...<br/>Those two were meant to be fo</span>
  <span id="freeText6375479179933243466" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>***5 "<u>My Brown Eyed Girl</u>" stars***</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465644461i/19383752._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>OMG!!! This book wrecked me, but i think that it will stay with me for a long time!!!<br>It was so difficult to witness this love...<br>It started at very young age and all those obstacles that were standing on their way were making my heart bleeding!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383753.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Alex and Lucas hurt each other very much and my heart was breaking for them...<br>They left other things to complicate their love and at the end they just making one mistake after the other...<br>Those two were meant to be forever together and i was dying inside that life was so unfair to them!!!<br>Seriously guys, i spent the last 70% crying like a baby...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415490253ra/11798907.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>But let me explain some things about their complicated love...</i><br><br><b>
  <i>"When you're that young, you don't realize how short life truly is. You think you will have all the time in the world to be and do whatever your heart desires. It will eventually get there; it's bound to happen. One day."</i>
</b><br><br>Alex, Lucas, Dylan, Jacob and Austin grew up together and they were bound with a unique friendship... Alex was their Half-pint, the glue that was stucking them together and the four boys were her <i>"Good Ol' Boys"</i>...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383754.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But Lucas was something more than just a friend for her and Alex was something more for Lucas as well...<br>From a very young age those two had a unique connection...<br>They were loving each other fiercely... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409632714ra/11001993.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>...but the circumstances and the people around them didn't leave them room to do what their hearts wanted to do...<br><br><b>
  <i>"They say you have that one moment in life where things could have been different, that one moment that changes the course of your life or the direction you could have taken. That one moment that could forever change you and everything you wanted to be true, everything you wanted to believe."</i>
</b><br><br>The prologue of this book, picked up immediately my interest since I understood that Lucas and Alex had a great love but she was about to bound her life with another man...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427325270ra/14262553.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And then, it took us back many, many years before at the age of 10 for Alex and 12 for Lucas...<br>We witness all the important moments of their life, all the love that they were feeling for each other, all the restraint because of others... <br>We saw them make one mistake after the other and how their choices affected their entire future...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423625450ra/13651996.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"She belonged to me. <br>Plain and simple. <br>Our emotions were running wild, trying to accept the bond our hearts will forever have. We laid our love out for each other years ago. I fought a battle I knew I could never win. The emotional turmoil ate away at me the closer we got to saying goodbye. That’s what happened when two halves of a heart come together and become one. <br>We would always be linked. <br>We were destined to be soul mates. <br>Star-crossed lovers."</i>
</b><br><br>Those two were meant to be together but life was so unfair to them...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383755.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>So will they manage to find their way back to each other???<br>Will they have their happily ever after???</i><br><br><b>
  <i>"I loved her. I knew I loved her, I always have and I always will. She owned every part of me. My heart was hers since before I knew what having her even meant."</i>
</b> <i>{Lucas}</i><br><br><b>
  <i>"It was only Lucas. <br>Always Lucas. <br>Not one other soul had this pull. <br>On me. <br>On him. <br>On us."</i>
</b> <i>{Alex}</i><br><br>I loved Lucas and Alex... Bo and his Half-pint!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383756.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I was living for the moments that they were together, but damn me, they hurt each other so much and mostly Lucas.... <br>But it wasn't his fault and that's why i was mad...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437217135ra/15550430.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Jacob and Dylan warned him all the goddamn time to stay away from her and their parents were saying to both of them that they had to experience life before they will bound theirs together, and that warnings-advices kept them away for very long time and the constant pressure from the guys to Lucas had awful results!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383757.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"The boy who promised he would never hurt her.<br>The boy who swore he would always protect her.<br>The boy who vowed he would never let anything happen to her.<br>That same boy was me.<br>I was the reason she was bawling.<br>I was the reason she was hurt.<br>I was the reason she was broken."</i>
</b><br><br>I loved Alex... She was sincere, wild, innocent, kind and very, very sweet...<br>She loved Lucas since she was remembering herself... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383758.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yep, she was a tom boy most of the time, but deep inside she was just a girl!!!<br>I know that she was very young and at that young age is impossible to know what love is, but while i was reading the book, it gave me the impression that the past was narrative... So, i personally could accept it!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380975725ra/3630786.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>As a girl, Alex was even harder to move on from Lucas... She was there for him all the time, with the hope that something will change between them, but at some point, it became really hard to loving him... It was hurting her so much!!! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383759.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But she kept doing it, no matter what!!! And i love her for that reason...<br><br><b>
  <i>"It overwhelmed me and consumed me. It hurt me and slayed me. Like a giant blade was driven directly in my heart."</i>
</b><br><br>I loved Lucas instantly... He was untamed, hotheaded and such a wonderful friend...<br>To Alex was always thoughtful, tender, possessive... He loved her fiercely and completely and that fact never changed even everything that happened between them...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383760.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Alex was the only person that could tame his wild soul... <br>And he was hurting so much when he was away from her, but everyone around him was pressuring him and he hurt her in an effort to let her free... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383761.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And that was his biggest regret!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>"You're a good girl, Alexandra. That's what makes you my Half-Pint. You're the calm to my storm; it's always been that way. You're my refuge."</i>
</b><br><br>I liked all the rest of the boys, but to be honest, i got mad with them... Especially with Jacob and Dylan... <br><i>Why??? Why they had to interfere in Alex's and Lucas relationsip??? Why, guys???</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383762.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I liked very much Austin and i'm dying for his turn to tell his story... He was such a troubled guy!!!<br>I also loved Aubrey, even though that i have so many questions about her and Dylan...<br>I adored little Lilly... She was a lovely girl!!! She was such a spitfire!!!<br>I hated Cole from the first moment... I didn't like the way that he was provoking Lucas and i hated that Alex wasted so much time with him!!!<br>Yeah, i know that he was charming, but still...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383763.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>I also was very angry with their both parents because they knew how much they loved each other, but in a way, they stood between them with bullshits!!!<br>But damn me, if i wasn't sad at the end with Lucas's mom... I couldn't see straight from the tears!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383764.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“If you would just tell her you loved her and wanted to be with her then… voilà,” she exclaimed with her hands out in the air. “Problem fixed.” <br>“There’s way more to it than that, kid.” <br>“Nah uh. Love is easy. It’s you that’s making it hard.”</i>
</b> <i>{Lilly-Lucas}</i><br><br>Well, as you can understand i loved that book even though that it hurt me deeply...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465644462ra/19383765.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>That's one of the things about me...<br>Everything that is hurting me, it will stay with me forever, and this story will be not an exception...<br>I'm already on the fourth book and i know that this one will be always one of my favorites...<br>Bo and his Half-pint will be always close to my heart!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460215500ra/18714380.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"When... when... when...<br>Our relationship was filled with what ifs, and maybe some days...<br>It was complicated. <br>It was messy. It was us. <br>I couldn't take her in small doses and I couldn't take her in large ones. Nothing was never enough."</i>
</b><br></span>

<div id="review_1383859864" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1383859864" />
    <a title="Kelli C " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c"><img alt="Kelli C " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1426900480p2/14931216.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1383859864?book_show_action=true">Sep 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelli C " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelli C " href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c">Kelli C </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=amazing">amazing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=must-reads">must-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=v-card-intact">v-card-intact</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=second-chance-love">second-chance-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=fab-writing">fab-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1383859864" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8826796799397165375">5 Brown Eyed Girl Stars!<br/><br/><i>*ARC provided in exchange for honest review*</i><br/><br/>Beautifully Broken. Heartbreakingly Complex. Poignant and Passionate. <i>Complicate Me</i> is a coming of age romance that weaves a lifetime of firsts into a future of forever. First friends, first loves, innocent kisses, first heartbreaks all set the foundation for two destined souls to take a long angst filled journey through adolescence into adulthood.<br/><br/><a href='http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1441591190624_zpsr0hf1gon.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441667652i/16135207.jpg' alt=' photo PhotoGrid_1441591190624_zpsr0hf1gon.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Alexandra, aka Half-pint, is one of the guys. Surrounded by 3 of the best guy </span>
  <span id="freeText8826796799397165375" style="display:none">5 Brown Eyed Girl Stars!<br><br><i>*ARC provided in exchange for honest review*</i><br><br>Beautifully Broken. Heartbreakingly Complex. Poignant and Passionate. <i>Complicate Me</i> is a coming of age romance that weaves a lifetime of firsts into a future of forever. First friends, first loves, innocent kisses, first heartbreaks all set the foundation for two destined souls to take a long angst filled journey through adolescence into adulthood.<br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1441591190624_zpsr0hf1gon.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441667652i/16135207.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1441591190624_zpsr0hf1gon.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Alexandra, aka Half-pint, is one of the guys. Surrounded by 3 of the best guy friends, she grows up loved and protected. Her biggest support comes from the arms of Lucas “Bo” Ryder. Two years her senior, he connects to her more than any other. Alex and Lucas has a special bond that grows with each passing year. “I Love You” is just the norm for the two…until those words seem to mean more. As each character grows up, the transition from girl to woman and boy to man is difficult for all. Jealousy, anger, insecurity, and new emotions of desire begin to filter into their lives. No one more affected than Alex and Lucas…<br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1441591597748_zpscuwstbmm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441667653i/16135208.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1441591597748_zpscuwstbmm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>No one said surviving your first love would be easy. With the age difference and the core group of family and friends against anything Alex and Lucas related, each try to grow into their own only knowing in their hearts what they truly want. Stolen moments, forehead kisses, words of claiming all present but not enough to overcome the trials and tribulations of growing up...<br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1441592992160_zpsjph1wfkm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441667653i/16135209.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1441592992160_zpsjph1wfkm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This story, while long and frustrating, was amazing. I loved the realism that the author brought to the read. Following a cast from childhood into adulthood is often difficult, but all those emotions associated with growing up compounded with falling in love and having your heart broken was so point on. It was a long and difficult journey for Alex and Lucas filled with moments of tender passion, pure adoration, and total devastation. Friends to Lovers? Never an easy thing. Can one’s soul mate be found riding the handlebars of a bike? Does a lifetime of friendship determine a future forever? How many times can the heart shatter before it is permanently broke? <br> <br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1441593271446_zps4rmc0yl0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441667653i/16135210.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1441593271446_zps4rmc0yl0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Perhaps it is Forgiveness at the heart of it all. Maturity is not just aging…it is accepting one’s self, owning the past, and grasping onto the future. This author did a stunning job of bringing two lives full circle. Thru ups and downs, love and loss, pleasure and pain, <i>Complicate Me</i> will leave you emotionally drained while giving your heart palpitations. I recommend this read to those lovers of angst, to those who have ever fell for the boy next door, for those who believe that first loves are forever loves! <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8826796799397165375" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1382060589" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1382060589" />
    <a title="Brandi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi"><img alt="Brandi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1384348451p2/5494655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1382060589?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=arc-netgalley-author">arc-netgalley-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1382060589" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17639231434904755252"><br/><b>2.5 Stars </b><br/><br/>I love angst. I enjoy emotional turmoil, the suffering, the heartache – it makes the resolution so much sweeter. That said, it only works if I connect with the characters – I need development, depth, I need to know them, to care about them and their story. Unfortunately, that is where <i>Complicate Me</i> missed the mark for me.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>We would always be linked. We were destined to be soul mates. Star-crossed lovers.</b>
</i><br/><br/>Growing up as an only child in a small coastal town, Alexandra develops a special</span>
  <span id="freeText17639231434904755252" style="display:none"><br /><b>2.5 Stars </b><br /><br />I love angst. I enjoy emotional turmoil, the suffering, the heartache – it makes the resolution so much sweeter. That said, it only works if I connect with the characters – I need development, depth, I need to know them, to care about them and their story. Unfortunately, that is where <i>Complicate Me</i> missed the mark for me.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>We would always be linked. We were destined to be soul mates. Star-crossed lovers.</b>
</i><br /><br />Growing up as an only child in a small coastal town, Alexandra develops a special bond with 4 local boys. She’s one of them, although 2 years younger; she is their little sisters, their ‘half-pint’. They are a tight knit group, caring deeply for each other, but for Alex and Lucas that bond is a bit stronger. As time progresses, Lucas and Alex struggle with their growing feelings for one another, an innocent bond turning into something neither of them really understands. This leads to years of push and pull, while caring deeply for one another, Lucas and Alex attempt to maintain their friendship. This is a coming of age story, full of firsts - crushes, kisses, dates, sex, heartbreak, love – all combining to tell an angsty love story. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>Our first kiss was our beginning and in some ways our end. This is where our complicated love began.</b>
</i><br /><br />Lucas and Alex’s relationship was just frustrating, their reasoning was confusing, and I honestly didn’t really like either of them. They were juvenile, selfish and most of the time unapologetic about it, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I was not a fan of how they used people - Stacey &amp; Cole. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <i>Complicate Me</i> also seemed to set up upcoming story lines in the series, which I found distracting, a lot was going on. I almost wish the author had written a novella introducing Alex and the boys, and started this novel with Alex being a bit older (she was 11-14 for a large portion of the story). Then maybe more time could be spent developing Alex and Lucas. I wanted to love this story, but overall it just didn't work for me. <br /><br /><br /><i>*ARC provided in exchange for an honest review* </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="17639231434904755252" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1376905740" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1376905740" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1376905740?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=dnf">dnf</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1376905740" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11619284086928128411"><b>No rating</b><br/><br/>Out of respect to the author, as I stopped at 52% and skimmed to the end, I won't rate this book.<br/><br/>I'm a self professed angst whore. I love it. I gobble it up and beg for more. I just love how it hurts SO good. Unfortunately for me, this book had angst, but it wasn't at all my cuppa. It had all the ingredients and perhaps if it was laid out different, it would have worked for me. So what didn't?<br/><br/>I did not realize that this book would take the reader year by year through the H/h lives start</span>
  <span id="freeText11619284086928128411" style="display:none"><b>No rating</b><br><br>Out of respect to the author, as I stopped at 52% and skimmed to the end, I won't rate this book.<br><br>I'm a self professed angst whore. I love it. I gobble it up and beg for more. I just love how it hurts SO good. Unfortunately for me, this book had angst, but it wasn't at all my cuppa. It had all the ingredients and perhaps if it was laid out different, it would have worked for me. So what didn't?<br><br>I did not realize that this book would take the reader year by year through the H/h lives starting from when the heroine is 10 and the hero 13. I can handle YA just fine, but what I don't want to read about is a 14 year old losing his virginity (in detail and not to the heroine), a first kiss when the heroine is 10 then 12, and the hero being for lack of a better word an utter douchebag simply because he's young and doesn't know any better. <br><br>I appreciated the idea behind it; truly engrossing the reader in the characters' journey through the years, but I'd have enjoyed it much more had these things been briefly mentioned through memory and not given to me detail by detail. It should have made me connect to the characters more, but it caused quite the opposite effect. I had no connection to the hero or the heroine. I saw no rhyme nor reason for most of the hero's actions aside from him being young and stupid. I'd rather it be hinted at that he's a manwhore than getting the blow by blow through the years, especially knowing he has zero feelings for the girl he's "getting it from" all the while pining for the heroine that he keeps systematically hurting with his actions. Perhaps if his actions made sense. Something other than peer pressure or him just being young. I don't even know. We all did stupid things at that age, but like I said, it doesn't mean I want to read about it. Perhaps most readers will write this off as "coming of age", but for me, there just wasn't a strong enough reason for anything the MCs did to justify it in my eyes. The character development simply wasn't strong enough for me to ever really connect. But again, this is solely a preference and other readers may have the complete opposite.<br><br>I think had this story started when the MCs were older, 17 or 18 even and then had some flashbacks to explain their relationship through the years..or maybe in the forms of brief memory descriptions...anything other than what it was. Maybe it's my mom brain kicking in, maybe it was something else. Whatever the case may be, it didn't work for me. There was also plot inconsistencies and some dialogue that was just plain weird. At one point one of the characters channeled his inner Larry the Cable Guy which had me scratching my head because these are supposed to be privileged rich kids. Who talks like that? Then again, this may just be my nitpicking since I was so withdrawn from the story.<br><br>I'm very much in the minority with my opinion and many others absolutely loved this book, so it really is a matter of subjective opinion. We all read differently and take things in differently. This is solely my opinion and it by no means suggests that you won't enjoy it. So read it and see for yourself.<br><br><br><i>ARC courtesy of author in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><b>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.com" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436477285i/15465455._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="11619284086928128411" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
