    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1386387274" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1386387274" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1386387274?book_show_action=true">Sep 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1386387274" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3512354949034326856"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442192668i/16201068._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Complicate Me</i> is the first story in the “Good Ol’ Boys Series” and I can honestly say without a doubt I am hooked. The story mostly focuses on Lucas and Alex, a boy and girl who have been friends their entire lives. However, the supporting cast is just as fantastic, I loved these boys and I am so intrigued and dying to read their stories. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>We would always be linked. We were destined to be soul mates. Star-crossed lovers.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>The story begins with us meeting Alex and Lucas as adolescents an</span>
  <span id="freeText3512354949034326856" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442192668i/16201068._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Complicate Me</i> is the first story in the “Good Ol’ Boys Series” and I can honestly say without a doubt I am hooked. The story mostly focuses on Lucas and Alex, a boy and girl who have been friends their entire lives. However, the supporting cast is just as fantastic, I loved these boys and I am so intrigued and dying to read their stories. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>We would always be linked. We were destined to be soul mates. Star-crossed lovers.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>The story begins with us meeting Alex and Lucas as adolescents and throughout the book we watch them grow up. From the beginning you can see that these characters are meant to be, but they are lack the maturity and their time is always off. While at times the story was very frustrating I was also able to understand and remind myself these are not adults and they don’t necessarily make the most mature decisions. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>They say you have that one moment in life where things could have been different, that one moment that changes the course of your life or the direction you could have taken. That one moment that could forever change you and everything you wanted to be true, everything you wanted to believe. </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Watching them grow up is seriously one of my favorite things of the story. It felt real to me. I loved seeing their trials, heart break and watching them grow as individuals. I think a lot of times we want the HEA and we want our heroes and heroines to be perfect, but my life and relationships have never been perfect, so I can relate more to these types of stories. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442192668i/16201069._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Alex is a tomboy and has always wanted to be “one of the guys” and for the most part is she, they protect her and make her feel like she belongs. But as they grow up things change and “her boys” change, they are no longer interested in building forts and hanging out, they are interested in girls. While they love her just the same their dynamic changes. <br><br>While all the guys love Alex, to Lucas she has always been his girl. Alex feels the same way about Lucas, but as they get older and start seeing each other in a different light everyone is against the idea of them together. Their parents want them to experience life and the guys think Alex deserves better than Lucas. These outside influences lead to a lot of heartbreak for them both, but it also allows them to see life without each other. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442192668i/16201070._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It’s safe to say this story will at times breaking your heart. I felt Alex’s pain and as a girl who was a tomboy I could completely relate to her. I completely fell in love with all the characters including the supporting characters. Although this is a longer story, the scenes felt necessary. I feel like the childhood, the build up all of that made me fall in love with their story. <br><br>This is my first book by M. Robinson and I can't wait to read more, I definitely recommend it. It’s not hearts and flowers, but it’s real, raw and emotional. There are moments you will want to throw your kindle, there are moments that made me cry, but in the end it’s worth it. As soon as I finished I wanted more! I cannot wait for Jacob’s story and to see what happens with his love interest. Long story short, I can easily see this series becoming a favorite and a must read for me.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Sometimes it takes leaving to know where you come from. To know where you belong.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review. </i>
</b><br><br>
  <a href="http://readingissexybookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574955.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
<br>
  <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Reading-is-Sexy-Book-Blog/717861984979600" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574956.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/13095060-beverly" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574957.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/readingissexybo/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574958.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=my-heart-can-barely-take-it">my-heart-can-barely-take-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=healing">healing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=high-angst-alert">high-angst-alert</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=not-what-i-expected">not-what-i-expected</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=second-chance-romance">second-chance-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1373243438" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4755733293731187763"> <b>~4 Love Can Be Complicated Stars~</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442772086i/16276894.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>"When you're that young, you don't realize how short life truly is. You think you will have all the time in the world to be and do whatever your heart desires. It will eventually get there; it's bound to happen. One day."-Lucas</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442776130ra/16277138.gif' width='400' height='50' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Complicate Me</b> is exactly what the title says~complicated! It is a story documenting the life and times of a group of friends stumbling through the awkward "coming of age" stage of life. It is the story of two of those friends who fell in l</span>
  <span id="freeText4755733293731187763" style="display:none"> <b>~4 Love Can Be Complicated Stars~</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442772086i/16276894.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"When you're that young, you don't realize how short life truly is. You think you will have all the time in the world to be and do whatever your heart desires. It will eventually get there; it's bound to happen. One day."-Lucas</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442776130ra/16277138.gif" width="400" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Complicate Me</b> is exactly what the title says~complicated! It is a story documenting the life and times of a group of friends stumbling through the awkward "coming of age" stage of life. It is the story of two of those friends who fell in love and didn't know what to do about it. When the pressure of doing what you are told is right or making the choice to be with the one you love is asked, what would you do?<br><br><b>"Our relationship was filled with what ifs, and maybe some days...it was complicated. It was messy. It was us. I couldn't take her in small doses and I couldn't take her in large ones."-Lucas</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442769452i/16276712.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Alex and Lucas grew up together in small town with a tight group of friends. Alex was the only girl in the group and "the baby" of the bunch. They spent summers swimming, surfing, riding bikes, playing tag, and just growing up. Not only is the crew close but their parents are close as well. As the group begins to age, Lucas realizes that he feels a little more than brotherly love for Alex. Although he is supposed to only love her as a sister, he realizes that in fact, he loves her for so much more. Alex and Lucas are so young. The boys in the group are older and as they begin to mature the pressures of growing up begins to weigh the group down. Although Lucas knows he has feelings for Alex, he recognizes that she is too young for him to act on it. Additionally, he feels pressure from his friends to love her like a sister and protect her. As all boys do (at that age), he meets other girls and experiences the triumphs and fails of all of the "firsts". He maintains his friendship with Alex but begins to explore. While everyone is growing up, Alex is left as a spectator on the sidelines.<br><br> <b>"You're a good girl, Alexandra. That's what makes you my Half-Pint. You're the calm to my storm; it's always been that way. You're my refuge."-Lucas</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442769452i/16276713.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Alex and Lucas maintain a close friendship. There is no doubt that they both have feelings for each other and yet the constant pressure from their friends (and parents) keep them from being together. The story really begins to take off when Alex grows up. All of a sudden Lucas feels a pressure in his heart that he hasn't felt before. Can he honestly sit by and watch "his brown eyed girl" be with someone else?<br><br><b>"She was mine. I didn't want to share her. Not with Cole. Not with anyone. How do you explain something you don't even understand?"-Lucas</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442776294ra/16277149.gif" width="400" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lucas and Alex experience heartbreak every step of the journey. The way that they feel for each other can't compete with the realities of life and in their life time is a bitch! Sometimes time is not on your side. Sometimes by doing what we think is right, we make mistakes and we loose the people that we love. When the damage is done, can we really go back and make everything ok?<br><br> <b>"It overwhelmed me and consumed me. It hurt me and slayed me. Like a giant blade was driven directly in my heart."-Alex</b><br><br>What happens when too much time is passed and too many mistakes have been made? Could it be too late to be with the one we love?<br><br><b>"I loved you then, I love you now, I'll love you always."-Lucas</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442769452i/16276714.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Overall, I truly enjoyed <b>Complicate Me</b>. Days later I am still pondering the journey these two characters experienced. Every time Lucas walked away to be with another girl, I cried with Alex. Every time I thought Lucas was going to declare his love for her but didn't, I wanted to throw my kindle against the wall. This writing is raw and offers an accurate depiction of life. Told in dual POV we experience "both sides of the story!" The friendships are thoroughly felt through the complex character development and intense situations. The sexual tension in this read is intense and the tender moments between Alex and Lucas left me breathless. I would definitely recommend this read to anyone that is drawn to emotional reads with a heavy dosage of angst. I am not going to lie...my stomach and heart hurt the entire time I was reading this book. Once I started it, I couldn't stop until I reached the end. The anxiety I felt for both characters was magnified with every new challenge they were forced to face. However difficult the journey, the final result was well worth it! My only complaint is that we didn't get more time with Alex and Lucas at the end. I can only hope this means we will see more of them in the rest of the series! This is my first M. Robinson read but it will not be my last. (Only now I know I need to get my tissues and favorite bottle of wine ready!) My kindle will be ready and waiting for more.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411280ra/807434.gif" width="400" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>~ARC graciously provided via author in exchange for an honest review!~<br><br>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><a href="http://craziesrusbookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434387282i/15214674._SX540_.jpg" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>

</a><br><br><b>TITLE:</b> Complicate Me<br><b>SERIES:</b> (The Good Ol' Boys, #1) <br><b>AUTHOR:</b> M. Robinson <br><b>GENRE:</b> Contemporary Romance<br><b>RELEASE DATE:</b> September 14th 2015<br><br><b>MY RATING: 5 BROWN EYED GIRL STARS</b> <br><br>I've read ALL of M. Robinson's books and have cray cray LOVED them so am really intrigued to see what journey she takes me on with this book..<br><br>I can not tell you how much I loved this book, god the feels, loved the story line, the characters just came to life, I lived, breathed this book, for me it was truly epic..I love books like this..ALot of backwards forwards shit goes on between Alex and Lucas but that's the diversity of their ages, this starts off in their younger teen years, alot of miscommunication, alot of missed opportunities, alot of tears and anguish but that's what made me love this book as much as I did, it conveyed the age set of these teens perfectly, the emotional turmoil as teenagers..It was repetitive but keep in mind it's coming from a teenagers perspective, the survival of a first love, the survival of all the hurts, the survival of just over coming a teenager..<br><br>FOUR FRIENDS (4 Boys) and ONE GIRL <br><br><b>Jacob</b> - Is the oldest in the group and takes on the role "Big Brother" where Alex is concerned.<br><b>Dylan</b> - Is the closest to Jacob than any of the other boys <br><b>Austin</b> - He is the shortest in the group, girls fawned over him because of his red hair and green eyes<br><b>Lucas</b> - Or Bo as Alex calls him, was born to lead and not to follow and a temper that no one can match<br><br>And then we have <b> ALex aka Half Pint </b> The little firecracker tomboy who loves her boys fiercely. But has an undeniable connection with her boy Bo aka Lucas<br><br><b>
  <i>Our relationship was filled with what ifs, and maybe somedays… It was complicated. It was messy. It was us.</i>
</b><br><br>The story starts off in their young teens (Alex eleven, Lucas thirteen ) and progresses as they move through the ages, I freaking love books like this, child hood friends, from friends to lovers..<br><br><i> “I love you, Half-Pint, you’re my best friend,” </i><br><br>This is where it all officially starts, the story of Lucas and Alex<br><br>I can not imagine how hard this would've been to write, jumping in the mind of a thirteen year old boy, capturing the emotions that at that age are so misunderstood, I think M Robinson has truly captured the essence of these characters..<br><br><i> He turned fourteen, and I swear he grew overnight, he started to look like a man… maybe not a man, but definitely not like the boy he used to be. </i><br><br>Loving the dynamics of the boys and their need to protect Alex like a sister, but by doing that they are stunting her life experiences as they aren't allowing her to grow into her own person..<br><br><i>
  <b> I would turn fourteen in a few weeks and I still didn’t have any life experiences outside of the boys. I hadn’t dated anyone, kissed anyone else, or even been on a date. </b>
</i><br><br><i> All the boys on the island were too scared to come near me because they knew I came with baggage. Four of them. </i> <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=29di6ue" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>On Lucas' fourteenth birthday he got egged on by The good Ol boys to lose his virginity, which he did to the school skank, not knowing that Alex knew exactly what was going down that night..<br><br><b> I shattered her illusion that I was hers. </b><br><br>That night changed things between these two..<br><br><b>
  <i> She’s just a girl, Half-Pint, just a fucking girl,” he breathed out, and I never wanted to punch him in the face as much as I did in that second. </i>
</b><br><br>A raw emotional story of coming of age, as they progress through the stages of life, a journey of discovery..such a beautifully written heartfelt story..<br><br>So as I've been reading this for some reason I've been Humming the lyrics (If I were a boy by Bounce) and it seems fitting Lucas just seems to take everything where Alex is concerned for granted, he wants his cake and wants to eat it too..<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2vah0rn" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1381131890" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1381131890" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10367112-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515708587p2/10367112.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1381131890?book_show_action=true">Sep 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/10367112-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=best-friends">best-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=beta-read">beta-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=coming-of-age">coming-of-age</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1381131890" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5433867718663196580"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448083506i/17093523.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review</i><br/><br/>Complicate Me by M. Robinson is a raw, poignant, touching read that weaves the elements of first love, friendship, second chances, life, and love. In this engrossing tale, M. Robinson enchants her readers on all facets of love from first love, heartbreak, anger, lust, jealousy, and healing. She shows her readers that LOVE is a simple word but hard to define. Can an innocent love blossomed to a forever kind of love? A blurred love? A complic</span>
  <span id="freeText5433867718663196580" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448083506i/17093523.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br>Complicate Me by M. Robinson is a raw, poignant, touching read that weaves the elements of first love, friendship, second chances, life, and love. In this engrossing tale, M. Robinson enchants her readers on all facets of love from first love, heartbreak, anger, lust, jealousy, and healing. She shows her readers that LOVE is a simple word but hard to define. Can an innocent love blossomed to a forever kind of love? A blurred love? A complicated love? So in this complicated tale of young love, can two soul mates finally realize that true love isn't meant to be easy? That love doesn't appear on command and it'll put you through hurdles but in the end, none of that will matter because it's about how you overcome these hurdles that will define your love. So can a complicated love be uncomplicated?<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/20471735273/in/photostream/" title="11903512_10103840911404583_2093197799_n" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441220124i/16079523._SY540_.jpg" width="533" height="800" alt="11903512_10103840911404583_2093197799_n" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>If you have read M. Robinson's previous books then you are aware that Complicate Me is very different from her other books. In her newest release, this book reads more of a Coming of Age and New Adult genre than her typical erotic romance novels. I was pleasantly surprised with this book because M. Robinson was able to showcase more of a deeper and richer meaning of love and friendship. First love has always been one of those trope that I instantly gravitate to since these stories are usually deep with emotions, meaning, depth and love. We read romance books because it can make us FEEL and in Complicate Me, it really puts readers on an roller-coaster of emotions. <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/21100517431/in/photostream/" title="#complicate_ me" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441220124i/16079521._SX540_.jpg" width="800" height="478" alt="#complicate_ me" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Complicate Me focus on a group of friends who grew up together and had their lives intertwined with each other. Each moment of their life was ingrained and built on their strong love for each other. And it so happens that Lucas and Alex took their friendship to another level because they shared a bond that united their souls and hearts to each other. Alex was the only girl in the group that consisted of Lucas, Dylan, Jacob and Austin. They were her boys and her family but Lucas was so different and so much more to her and the same goes for him as well. If Lucas and Alex loved each other so much then how could their love be complicated?<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/20904926118/in/photostream/" title="#Complicate!Me_meesh" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441220124i/16079522._SX540_.jpg" width="800" height="499" alt="#Complicate!Me_meesh" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Their love was complicated because like any young person, feelings were never properly expressed since they were both afraid to ruin the friendship and dynamics of the group. But what happens when Lucas and Alex finally had the chance to make it right, unexpected news and misunderstandings tears to destroy their chance at love. Can their love get any more complicated when their future and life choices seems to put a hindrance at their chance of love? <br><br>Lucas and Alex relationship can only be summed up as roller-coaster. These two really puts you on an emotional ride of where at times I wanted to slap each of them upside the head and tell them to get their acts together but a part of me understood how young they were and they had a lot of growing up to do. As much as this story was focused on love, I think their foundation of friendship is what really draws and captures the reader's attention because their friendship is what made their love palpable. <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/20906788799/in/dateposted/" title="#complicateMe_4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441222509i/16079754.jpg" width="500" height="302" alt="#complicateMe_4" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Complicate Me is a book that raises a lot of complicated questions. Does years of friendship automatically mean that you are meant to be with that person? When love gets blurred and misunderstood, can it be easily fixed? Do first love and soul mates even exist? Can a love that was already complicated be uncomplicated? Though this book may have you questioning the relationship and status of Lucas and Alex, it really showcases that love just can't be defined and answered with a simple yes or no. The matters of the heart can only be answered by the two people who are involved in the equation. And for Lucas and Alex, their love was a solid foundation of growth and learning. Learning to let go, learning to forgive, learning to understand, learning of maturity, and most importantly learning to really love. So if you are looking for a love story that is filled with angst, drama, friendship and love, then I recommend you to give Complicate Me a try.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440184922r/15942327.jpg" width="306" height="68" alt="3f247b9b671b804756c0f608eeada2" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Review can also be found on Four Chicks Flipping Pages: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://fourchicksflippingpages.weebly.com">http://fourchicksflippingpages.weebly...</a></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="5433867718663196580" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Together with three other boys, they were as close as blood relatives, growing up together in the beach town of Oak Island, North Carolina. <br/><br/>But growing up wasn’t easy when attractions started to get in the way of innocent friendship. Sometimes, it took learning th</span>
  <span id="freeText288986652595025886" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444050957i/16446519.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Win ebook copy of Complicate Me!<br>Open Oct 5-9 only!<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://wp.me/p5bsdH-P7">http://wp.me/p5bsdH-P7</a></b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423265644i/13602509.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Type: </b> Standalone Book 1 of The Good Ol' Boys series<br><b>POV: </b> First Person - Dual<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424140745i/13720990.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441955930i/16173156.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lucas Ryder and Alexandra Collins had been best friends since they were born. Together with three other boys, they were as close as blood relatives, growing up together in the beach town of Oak Island, North Carolina. <br><br>But growing up wasn’t easy when attractions started to get in the way of innocent friendship. Sometimes, it took learning the hard way to appreciate what you have right in front of your eyes. The choices they made changed the course of the lives in ways they could never predicted. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423265644i/13602509.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br>I started this book totally blind only with the knowledge that it’s supposed to be angsty. I was pleasantly surprised it was a coming of age story. Such childhood innocence has always been something dear to my heart and I certainly enjoyed this one.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “I loved you then, I love you now, I’ll love you always.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I love Lucas or Bo since the beginning. There’s just something that made me gravitate towards him even when he was being an ass. And believe me he was an ass pretty much the whole book lol!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You push me aside when you want, but I’m here when you need me. I’m like your own personal play toy.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The above quote perfectly summed up Alex or Hal-Pint (love that nickname). She was a loyal friend and it’s sad it took her so long to realize her role in the relationship and did something about it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>We tend to hurt the ones we love. I had to learn that the hard way.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>If you love seeing your characters suffer emotionally, this book had plenty of that. They kept hurting each other purposely or accidentally – and people around them too. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441955930i/16173157.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What I love the most about this book is how we got to see the characters’ growing pains – not only the two main one, but also the rest of the gang. They started as a bunch of cute pre-teens and along the way the loss of innocence and the breakdown of their life/friendship were really sad. It made me wish they never grow up so they don’t have to suffer. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I had to let her grow up, but it didn’t mean I had to fucking like it.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The book started really well with the powerful prologue. But as the story progressed, I encountered some issues. The story plateaued for a while until the appearance of a new character. The push and pull needed some strong jolt to keep it interesting. <br><br>Also, I didn’t favor the constant reminder of something bad going to happen. As a reader, I like to experience it as I go along, instead of being told what to expect. And there were also the over usage of ellipses (I had to Google to know what it’s called haha!). It got tiring when it happened almost at the end (some in middle too) of each POV. <br><br>Complicate Me follows the life journey of two individuals and their best friends from childhood to adult stringing readers along with their love and heartbreaks. You’ll laugh with them, swoon for them and cry for them and wish you have them in your life. <br><br><i><b>Note:</b><br>I already have a soft spot for Austin. Tortured soul is my ultimate favorite. Looking forward to his story.</i><br> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437991042i/15653385.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:<br><a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412943984i/11445453.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415355089i/11776478.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1390581325" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1390581325" />
    <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts"><img alt="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591195447p2/16496589.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1390581325?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts">Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1390581325" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17716704520798398512"><br/>It's LIVE! * <a href='http://amzn.to/1Kh8vug' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon</a> * <a href='https://www.smashwords.com/books/view/576941' rel='nofollow noopener'>Smashwords</a> * <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442444187i/16234644.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>My feelings regarding COMPLICATE ME, for want of a better word, are quite complicated. On the one hand I loved the characters and premise, and towards the end I felt the intended emotion but in contrast there are times when the story did not hold my attention. It has all the ingredients that I love in my reading material, angst, slow build, great characters, romance and a love triangle but unfortunately these elements did not always gel cohesively for my person</span>
  <span id="freeText17716704520798398512" style="display:none"><br>It's LIVE! * <a href="http://amzn.to/1Kh8vug" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a> * <a href="https://www.smashwords.com/books/view/576941" rel="nofollow noopener">Smashwords</a> * <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442444187i/16234644.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My feelings regarding COMPLICATE ME, for want of a better word, are quite complicated. On the one hand I loved the characters and premise, and towards the end I felt the intended emotion but in contrast there are times when the story did not hold my attention. It has all the ingredients that I love in my reading material, angst, slow build, great characters, romance and a love triangle but unfortunately these elements did not always gel cohesively for my personal reading tastes. By the end, however, this author captured me with the emotion of her characters; it turned full circle for me and the last 20% of this book I devoured. <br><br>It's about a group of friends who've known each other forever, a group of boys and one girl. The story begins at a place in time when the heroine is ten and the hero is a little older. It's a friends to lovers story with elements of unrequited love and a love triangle as the protagonists navigate their way haphazardly through their life, making mistakes and growing up. The premise really ticks my reading preferences but I feel it was fleshed out too extensively in the earlier years. There are elements that felt repetitive in word or emotion which affects the pace and flow of the story. Time transitions ere not always smooth and clear and I didn’t always fully buy into the motivation that drove the story. This led to feelings of frustration rather than angst. <br><br>Lucas our hero appears quite selfish and week in much of the story which is not an attractive quality. It could be a result of his youth and immaturity but, to me, it felt more than this. Interestingly I still warmed to him as a book hero, faults and all. It took me longer than it usually does, a good three quarters of the book, but in the end I admired him and I felt warm emotion towards him, his character undoubtedly develops considerably. Alex, the heroine, is strong and mature for her years. I like the way she conducts herself throughout the story and always had hopes for her happy-ever-after.<br><br>Despite my conflicted feelings and the fact that I even skimmed in places, I felt committed to discovering the final fate of Lucas and Alex, having become quite attached to them despite certain aspects not appealing to me. The angst overload clearly had a positive affect on me in the end, I would go even further than this and say the last 20% really captured my affection, made me well up with emotion and, despite my previous skimming; I was completely invested and read it avidly.<br><br><br>****Do they live happily ever after? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <br><br>Advanced copy provided by the author, via Like a Boss Book Promotions and Blog, in exchange for my honest review thoughts<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1555456297" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1555456297?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1555456297" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13217574273688752131">I don't even know where to begin with this book!! Holy smoly, what an emotional roller coaster ride this was, and when I say this I am not saying it lightly. The thing with this story is that it has a few of my pet peeves in it; but even with my peeves...I was hooked. In fact, I can honestly say that I haven't got a lot done since I started this book!! <br/><br/>Complicate me is the start of "The Good Ol' Boys" series, and it is about a group of friends who grow up together in a small town. Alexandra is t</span>
  <span id="freeText13217574273688752131" style="display:none">I don't even know where to begin with this book!! Holy smoly, what an emotional roller coaster ride this was, and when I say this I am not saying it lightly. The thing with this story is that it has a few of my pet peeves in it; but even with my peeves...I was hooked. In fact, I can honestly say that I haven't got a lot done since I started this book!! <br /><br />Complicate me is the start of "The Good Ol' Boys" series, and it is about a group of friends who grow up together in a small town. Alexandra is the only girl in the group, and is the youngest...the boys nick-named her "Half-pint" and she did everything she could to keep up with "HER" boys! There is one boy in particular though, that has an extra special bond with Alex, his name is Lucas...aka..."Bo."<br /><br />As they continue to grow up, they develop a bond that is more and more solid. The thing is that Bo is a few years older than HIS Half-pint, and he ends up trying to be noble and not touch her, as he should view her more like his sister. Over the whole book though, Bo spends his time having sex with a ton of girls that are not her, and ends up hurting her more and more, until their relationship is very damaged. This is where my pet peeve begins...actually; that is a lie...my peeve stepped in the first time Lucas slept with another girl who wasn't Alex. I was furious...but as I said in the beginning of my review, even being angry, I couldn't not read this story. I just had to find out how it was going to go.<br /><br />I will be honest in this review and warn readers that for most of the book this couple isn't together. They spend a lot of time apart, and a lot of time fighting their attraction for one another, or hurting one another. Somehow though, the author brilliantly writes a story that does keep you glued to the pages, and even enjoying this solid bond that all of these friends share. It also has you sit back and think about life in general, and how one little mistake, or one turn in a road can take us on a whole new direction in life. This is a book that will make you stop and think, it will have you laughing, crying, and even wanting to throw your kindle across the room. It is a perfect book for readers who love a lot of angst in a story. <br /><br />I'd love to say that I won't put myself through anymore misery and read more of this series...but I'd be lying. In fact, I have already started on book two! These childhood friends, all have a story of their own, and I'm sure they are all full of heartache too. I guess deep down I am a sucker for punishment!!! I am hooked and I have to pray that they will all find their HEA...Or as little sister Lily would say: "I have to find my lobster!!!"</span>
  <a data-text-id="13217574273688752131" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText7612574657122461794" style="display:none">I was literally placed in a boxing ring while I read this book. <div id="review_1391421118" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1391421118" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1391421118?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13126896-michelle?shelf=01-signed">01-signed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1391421118" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6291865183068365550">Okay so more often than not, I find myself reading a book, finishing it and then waiting till the weekend to gather my thoughts and reviewing. But with this book, that formula is just <b>not</b> going to work. So I'm just going to let my emotions create havoc here and hope that it some how makes sense.<br/><br/>Complicate Me is a gripping coming of age romance that pairs up Lucas and Alex. Our two main characters that have known each other since birth. Two best friends. Two souls that become lost in the storm th</span>
  <span id="freeText6291865183068365550" style="display:none">Okay so more often than not, I find myself reading a book, finishing it and then waiting till the weekend to gather my thoughts and reviewing. But with this book, that formula is just <b>not</b> going to work. So I'm just going to let my emotions create havoc here and hope that it some how makes sense.<br><br>Complicate Me is a gripping coming of age romance that pairs up Lucas and Alex. Our two main characters that have known each other since birth. Two best friends. Two souls that become lost in the storm that swirls around them as they grow, experience life and wait for all the destruction to settle.<br><br>The prologue of this story sets the tone flawlessly. We first meet Lucas and Alex on a beach sharing a stolen moment that held so much emotion, so much pain and yet you could just feel the love that burned so damn bright. And as we begin the journey. M. Robinson takes us to the very beginning with two kids. One girl that wants to be anything but a girl and her boys, the men that would protect her through her youth, learn to let go as she blossomed and one special best friend that would constantly break and fill her heart. <br><br>Although the majority of this story takes place as these kids grow up, the story still held such tension between the characters. Their story so much more mature than what two teenagers share. We journey from first kisses, first tears, first heartbreaks and the many that would follow. <br><br>I loved this book. The angst kept me on the edge of my seat and my heart broke over and over again for Alex and Lucas as they faced growing up and learning that their actions had consequences. Consequences that led to suffering. At times "Bo" and "Half-Pint" had me laughing and smiling but the emotional pull that I felt towards these two often left me a sobbing mess. I wanted to reach into this book and hug-shake them so hard. <br><br>It's been about an hour after I finished this and I still feel so overwhelmed by the feelings this story evoked. Everything about this story just flowed so naturally, nothing over done or undone, just absolute perfection. I fell in love with every character that was introduced in this first book. Each one of them claimed a piece of me. And this is one of those books that I know months, years from now will cross my mind and make me smile and get a little choked up all at the same time. <br><br>Complicate Me is the first in the Good Ol' Boys Series and is a standalone (each book will feature one of the boys) and is a complete must read. <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/15250834182" title="ARC by Book Worm, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410813673i/11155676.jpg" width="400" height="166" alt="ARC" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6291865183068365550" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1624005088" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1624005088" />
    <a title="Dilek VT" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt"><img alt="Dilek VT" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448923258p2/49572641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1624005088?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dilek VT" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dilek VT" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt">Dilek VT</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=deep-emotions">deep-emotions</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=heartache">heartache</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=torturing-in-a-beautiful-way">torturing-in-a-beautiful-way</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=successful-writing">successful-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=love-drama">love-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=friendship">friendship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=angst-and-drama">angst-and-drama</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1624005088" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9375759618273633410">This is the 1st book in the GOOD OL’ BOYS series. The series tell the stories of a bunch of childhood friends: Alexandra and her boys, Lucas, Jacob, Dylan and Austin... <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462126348i/18956973._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462126348i/18956974._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The 1st book in the series is about two of them: Lucas and Alexandra. The 2nd book is about Jacob and Lucas’s sister, Lily, the 3rd book is about Dylan, and the 4th book is about Austin. Although they are each stand-alone books with no cliff-hanger, each one contains information about these people so it is better if you read them</span>
  <span id="freeText9375759618273633410" style="display:none">This is the 1st book in the GOOD OL’ BOYS series. The series tell the stories of a bunch of childhood friends: Alexandra and her boys, Lucas, Jacob, Dylan and Austin... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462126348i/18956973._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462126348i/18956974._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The 1st book in the series is about two of them: Lucas and Alexandra. The 2nd book is about Jacob and Lucas’s sister, Lily, the 3rd book is about Dylan, and the 4th book is about Austin. Although they are each stand-alone books with no cliff-hanger, each one contains information about these people so it is better if you read them in order not to be confused by the bits of hints and spoilers.<br><br>I started this first book “Complicate Me”, knowing that a great portion of the book was about when they were 10, 12, 14 years old and I also thought I might be bored and may have to skip a little bit at the beginning because of that. Wow, I couldn’t be more wrong! The book captured my attention first in the prologue, which is when they are twenty something years old and then I really couldn’t put it down wondering how things went there. <br><br>All these childhood and teenage years are told in such a beautiful way that, let alone skipping, I read some pages twice or three times with bloody tears in my eyes. The whole book, the story in it is so emotional. The tone of the writing is so effective that from the first page on, I felt as if the writer has taken my heart in her hands and slowly squeezed the life out of it along with the non-stop heartache the story caused. The angst, the sorrows and the pain gradually rose and only after %95 of the book, the cheerful tone began and I was rewarded a happy end as a survival gift after all that suffering!<br><br>***<br><br>Alexandra/Alex or as the boys call, Half-Pint is a tom boy and when a little child, she didn’t like any girl-stuff. She always played with the boys, acted and dressed like them. She was their friend, their little sister and she was the glue in their friendship, as the following years showed.<br><br>She loved all these boys but one was always closer to her heart: Lucas, or as she called him, Bo…<br>For Lucas, it was no different. She was his “Brown-eyed girl”. Even before she was born, she was his. This is what his mother says:<br><i>
  <b><br>"My boy has been smitten with you since the moment you were born. I remember when your mama was pregnant, he would go up to her belly and say that it was his baby in there.”<br></b>
</i><br>As years passed, they slowly grew up. The boys were two years older than Alexandra, except for Austin, who was one year older. When teenage years came, the boys became guys and their bodies changed and so did their needs. When they started to become interested in girls, Alex took it so hard – she had no other friends other than the boys. And that is when the problems started. <br><br>Lucas and Alex had a special bond, they loved each other more than the others but they were young, so very young and they had so many things to experience with and without each other. While doing so, while fighting with the odds of growing up, they hurt each other badly...<br><i>
  <b><br> “I shattered her illusion that I was hers.”<br><br>***<br><br>“The boy who promised he would never hurt her.<br>The boy who swore he would always protect her.<br>The boy who vowed he would never let anything happen to her.<br>That same boy was me.<br>I was the reason she was bawling.<br>I was the reason she was hurt.<br>I was the reason she was broken.”<br><br>***<br><br>“I had to let her grow up, but it didn’t mean I had to fucking like it.” <br><br>***<br><br> “I would turn fourteen in a few weeks and I still didn’t have any life experiences outside of the boys. I hadn’t dated anyone, kissed anyone else, or even been on a date. All the boys on the island were too scared to come near me because they knew I came with baggage. Four of them.”<br><br>***<br><br>"It overwhelmed me and consumed me. It hurt me and slayed me. Like a giant blade was driven directly in my heart."<br><br>***<br><br>"She was mine. I didn't want to share her. Not with Cole. Not with anyone. How do you explain something you don't even understand?"<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462127960i/18957189.jpg" width="420" height="550" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>“Our first kiss was our beginning and in some ways our end. This is where our complicated love began.”<br></b>
</i><br>Well, if you ask me, <b>“falling in love with your childhood friend while growing up”</b> sucks because you have a long time to grow up and experience life, trying to understand what you want in life, what you want to be, where you want to live and how you can be happy etc. and committing to someone at the teenage years is not healthy because then, in the following years, you may have lots of doubts about your commitment if not resentment.<br><b><br>AND THAT IS WHY, </b>Alex and Lucas suffered… and they suffered a lot… <br><br>They had to go through all this hurt, the angst and the come-and-go between them…<br><br>They also had to deal with all the people interfering, the boys, the families, other girls, other boys, all playing their part in separating the two of them. They all complicated the things between Alex and Lucas.<br><br>Oh boy, they had to endure a lot...<br><br>But they had this unbelievable connection –this strong bond... always...<br><i>
  <b><br>“The feelings I had, what he provoked and stirred within me, what he always did to me. No one could ever explain or understand what it was. How it happened. No one else could do this. It was only Lucas. Always Lucas. Not one other soul had this pull. On me. On him. On us.” <br><br>***<br><br>“We would always be linked. We were destined to be soul mates. Star-crossed lovers.”<br></b>
</i><br>Some reasons and plot twists made sense, some were too annoying for me, lots of miscommunication and missed opportunities, bad timing etc. but all in all, they all happened for a reason as we saw in the end. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462142522i/18958612._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b><br>“We have so many barriers placed in between us and I don’t know how to remove them.” <br><br>***<br><br>"Love shouldn’t hurt this much. All you’ve ever done… is complicate me.”<br></b>
</i><br>Bookylicious and I did a buddy-read and we both cried our eyes out while reading it but anyways, we fell in love with this beautiful book. <br><br>It is told from alternate point of views, both Alex and Lucas’s and the Prologue sticks a sharp knife in your heart, followed by all those chapters in which the knife turns and twists all the time giving you more and more pain until the last few chapters and a very happy Epilogue.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462126348i/18956976._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you ask me, don’t miss this book if you are a romance reader. It was worth 5 stars and many more... It was an epic read...<br><br><br><br><br> <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="9375759618273633410" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1376523661" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1376523661" />
    <a title="Mary Elizabeth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5872215-mary-elizabeth"><img alt="Mary Elizabeth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600918968p2/5872215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1376523661?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mary Elizabeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mary Elizabeth" href="/user/show/5872215-mary-elizabeth">Mary Elizabeth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1376523661" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2272379879324896638">Five “be still my heart” stars! <br/><br/>Complicate Me is my first book from M. Robinson. Known for penning sensual erotica novels, this coming-of-age story is Robinson’s first in the Young adult/ New Adult genre. I have no doubt the readership will welcome her with open arms. <br/><br/>As both a reader and author of coming-of-age books, they are tricky to pull off, and more often than not fall flat if not carefully constructed. Most adults are not going to want to read about small children coloring on the walls, </span>
  <span id="freeText2272379879324896638" style="display:none">Five “be still my heart” stars! <br /><br />Complicate Me is my first book from M. Robinson. Known for penning sensual erotica novels, this coming-of-age story is Robinson’s first in the Young adult/ New Adult genre. I have no doubt the readership will welcome her with open arms. <br /><br />As both a reader and author of coming-of-age books, they are tricky to pull off, and more often than not fall flat if not carefully constructed. Most adults are not going to want to read about small children coloring on the walls, but if the reader is anything like me, they do want to read about love at first sight, even if it’s from filthy-faced kids. That is what we get with Alexandra “Half-Pint” and Lucas “Bo.” <br /><br />This “complicated” love story starts when they are younger, but takes us through their heart wrenching journey into adulthood. This tale is in no shortage of angst, but what I was most impressed with was the believable self-discovery and progression I experienced with all of the characters. They don’t make the right choices every time, but it’s believable and it’s relatable. M. Robinson includes great detail without boring the reader, and writes in such a way that even when we want to hate someone, we easily forgive and forget. And trust me, there’s a lot of forgiving. <br /><br />I don’t think unputdownable is a word, but it describes Complicate Me perfectly. <br /><br />Alex and Lucas are unputdownable! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2272379879324896638" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2366905135" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2366905135" />
    <a title="Hanne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21725822-hanne"><img alt="Hanne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1456934758p2/21725822.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2366905135?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hanne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hanne" href="/user/show/21725822-hanne">Hanne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21725822-hanne?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2366905135" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13675920047806428101">Alexandra (or Alex like she wants to be called), Lucas and three other boys are best friends since they were little. Alex has always been one of the guys, but she didn’t mind that at all. Alex and Lucas’ friendship is closer than her friendship with the other boys. When Alex is a little older, she starts to have romantic feelings for Lucas. Lucas also wants more than friendship, but he thinks she’s too young. Over the next couple of years, Lucas dates a few women and Alex remains single. Lucas a</span>
  <span id="freeText13675920047806428101" style="display:none">Alexandra (or Alex like she wants to be called), Lucas and three other boys are best friends since they were little. Alex has always been one of the guys, but she didn’t mind that at all. Alex and Lucas’ friendship is closer than her friendship with the other boys. When Alex is a little older, she starts to have romantic feelings for Lucas. Lucas also wants more than friendship, but he thinks she’s too young. Over the next couple of years, Lucas dates a few women and Alex remains single. Lucas and Alex always keep being best friends, until one day they aren’t.<br /><br />I didn’t connect with the characters and I got frustrated with them a lot. If I have to choose between Alex and Lucas, I’ll pick Alex. She’s sweet and loving, but she can be naïve and she waited too long for Lucas. Lucas slept around for too long and that’s not something you do when you want someone. He knew he hurt her, but he kept doing it. Lucas did change when he went to college, but it was too late for me. I do like the secondary characters enough to try the next books in this series, but I’ll quit reading if I don’t like them.<br /><br />I knew from the prologue that there was hurt and a past between Lucas and Alex and I couldn’t wait to know more about those characters. After a while I couldn’t root for Alex and Lucas anymore. There was too much hurt and stupid decisions. It took way too long for them to be together. I just wished that Lucas or Alex said ‘Let’s no longer care what everybody says and let’s proof to them that we can be together forever’ sooner. I did like those last couple of chapters when they finally were a couple. A part of both of them always loved the other, and they will always love each other.<br /><br />I didn’t like Complicate Me. I finished this book because I needed to know when and how Alex and Lucas would end up being a couple. I start to like the book more when Lucas went to college, but it was too late. There were some good moments, but there were more bad moments.<br /><br />I did a buddy read with Chan. I’m glad we agreed on so much! I was super excited about our buddy read, but let’s pick a better book next time lol.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13675920047806428101" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1577737303" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/45826136-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1523893682p2/45826136.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1577737303?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/45826136-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45826136-katerina?shelf=one-star-dnf-pile">one-star-dnf-pile</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1577737303" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7338878891258791362">I hated this book. That is the plain and simple truth. <br/><br/>There's too much angst, too much stupidity, wayyyy too much emotional cheating. Cheating doesn't only occur when you are in a definitive named relationship of boyfriend-girlfriend or husband-wife. It can happen when you know you are in an emotional loving relationship without a label. <br/><br/>Lucas and Alexandra have been in a relationship from the start of their friendship. Fair enough she is two years younger than him, but if he really loved her? </span>
  <span id="freeText7338878891258791362" style="display:none">I hated this book. That is the plain and simple truth. <br /><br />There's too much angst, too much stupidity, wayyyy too much emotional cheating. Cheating doesn't only occur when you are in a definitive named relationship of boyfriend-girlfriend or husband-wife. It can happen when you know you are in an emotional loving relationship without a label. <br /><br />Lucas and Alexandra have been in a relationship from the start of their friendship. Fair enough she is two years younger than him, but if he really loved her? The wait should have been worth it. <br /><br />Instead we get this: <br /><br />•Lucas sleeping around.<br />•Having sex with every girl within vicinity<br />•Consoling Alexandra when she's upset saying "She's just a girl. I love you." (Overtime it became a watered down phrase)<br />•Holding double standards and not letting Alex flirt with a guy or have any friendships. <br /><br />There's too much hypocritical slut shaming. Stacey/Britney is a name used all the time for those "bitch cheerleading man-stealing" girls. Lucas has sex with Stacey (spoiler—um not really) and eventually yes, this bitch will get pregnant if you keep using her and you don't put on fucking protection. Annoyed the hell out of me. Then he has the audacity to say she's a whore, and "trapped him" when she (again spoiler alert—I think not) gets pregnant. <br /><br />Things which have really started to annoy me with angsty books is now that whilst you go in for the tumultuous ride and expect a happy ending, children are being thrown into the mix which messes up the whole thing. <br /><br />One thing most readers NEED is for the child to be from the OTP. TOGETHER. Not from Stacy. Because then you get this:<br /><br />***<br />“Jesus Christ, Alex,” Aubrey yelled, running into my bedroom. “What’s going on?”<br />“It hurts! It hurts, Aubrey, it hurts so bad!” I crumbled to the ground and she came with me.<br /><br />“What? What hurts? Are you okay?” she panicked, trying to comfort me as I sat on my knees with my body hunched over.<br /><br />“I’m trying to keep from dying… I’m just trying to keep from dying,” I bawled, big, huge ugly tears.<br /><br />***<br /><br />And you get this:<br /><br />***<br /><br />"I never said life was fair.”<br /><br />“I hate it every time you say that.”<br /><br />“It doesn’t make it any less true, because if it were, you’d be the mother of my son and that ring on your finger would have been placed there by me.”<br /><br />^^^<br /><br />DO I WANT HIM TO DIE? Yes I fucking want him to die. <br /><br />If Lucas was a dog in heat all he should have done was made out with a few girls during high school. Waited it out until Alex turned at least 13. A 15 year old and 13 year old hooking up should be fine on both sides. And bang! They have a relationship. Instead we get "She's too young"... And "I can't wait"... "This is wrong."<br /><br />GIVE ME A FREAKIN' BREAK. <br /><br />He didn't deserve her. And you know what... I didn't even like her. In what life was she a tom-boy? <br /><br />Why do authors think that we always want a virgin girl (very limited experience), and a guy who can't keep it in his pants as a protagonist. I literally started to spaz out. We were as an audience invested into their relationship from when they were kids. That crap only works if they have JUST met and the bad-boy reforms. All of it HAPPENED whilst he knew her and was IN LOVE with her and HURT her. <br /><br />And he actually has the right to feel upset when she informs him that she's lost her virginity. She waited, and waited and offered and waited, he went off to college and she still waited. Well... What's a girl to do? Wait while you swerve your way through every p*ssy in town. <br /><br />I felt as if there were some underlying sexist comment the whole way through too. <br /><br />The way Dylan treated girls like trash and they still wanted him desperately, enjoying being treated like crap. When Austin's on ecstasy and only Alexandra( is it because she's a woman?) worries about him OD'ing and the rest are just like 'meh- it's a guy thing'. Or how Lucas had the whole "just-sex" thing and girls seduced him in anyway they could, throwing themselves at him with their slutty dresses and made up faces. It's not like that in real life. MOST girls are definitely not like that. <br /><br />Jacob is another one who is wishy-washy. Alexandra says to Jacob:<br /><br />***<br />"I don’t want some skanky girl like the ones you’re used to dating."<br />***<br /><br />What is a "skank" Alexandra?<br /><br />Or when a guy can swear but a girl can't?! <br /><br />***<br />“Fuck the law,” she let out.<br /><br />Jacob was over to her in two strides. “I will not tell you again. Watch your fucking mouth.”<br /><br />***<br /><br />GRRR.<br /><br />Cole is a great guy. I hated both her and Lucas. At times it felt as if the author was trying to paint Cole in a bad light but if the story was from his POV everything he said and was feeling would be completely justified and heartbreaking because of his unrequited love.<br /><br />The foreshadowing thing was annoying too in the narrative. It's dual POV and riddled with phrases like:<br /><br />I should have known<br />That was the last time <br />I wish I told him <br />Except that's all they were now<br />I would never know how much<br />I would learn soon enough how right I was.<br /><br />BORE. Etc etc etc<br /><br />1/5 stars. Bullshitometer too high. <br /><br />And I've read angsty books full of characters which I can love. These kids just didn't deserve their ever after.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7338878891258791362" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
